# Prometheus Web UI Authentication Implementation

Based on the provided GitHub repository content, I cannot locate specific Go files implementing web UI authentication mechanisms like BasicAuth middleware, TLS client certificate validation, or admin API access control within the displayed README and repository structure.

The repository shows these relevant directories:
- `/web` - Contains web UI components
- `/cmd` - Command-line tools
- `/config` - Configuration handling

However, the actual implementation files aren't detailed in the content provided. To find authentication-related code, you would need to:

1. **Explore the `/web` directory** directly on GitHub for HTTP handler implementations
2. **Check `/cmd/prometheus`** for server setup and middleware configuration
3. **Review the full source** at [github.com/prometheus/prometheus](https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus) by navigating to specific Go files

The README mentions that "Prometheus will now be reachable at http://localhost:9090/" but doesn't document built-in authentication mechanisms in the visible sections. Authentication features may be handled through reverse proxies or external tools rather than native implementation.

For definitive answers, inspect the actual `.go` files in the web and cmd directories rather than relying on README documentation.

   603→		w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
   604→	}))
   605→
   606→	return h
   607→}

  2026→func (api *API) deleteSeries(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
  2027→	if !api.enableAdmin {
  2028→		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorUnavailable, errors.New("admin APIs disabled")}, nil, nil}
  2029→	}
  2030→	if err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {
  2031→		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("error parsing form values: %w", err)}, nil, nil}
  2032→	}
  2033→	if len(r.Form["match[]"]) == 0 {
  2034→		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, errors.New("no match[] parameter provided")}, nil, nil}
  2035→	}
  2036→
  2037→	start, err := parseTimeParam(r, "start", MinTime)
  2038→	if err != nil {
  2039→		return invalidParamError(err, "start")
  2040→	}
  2041→	end, err := parseTimeParam(r, "end", MaxTime)
  2042→	if err != nil {
  2043→		return invalidParamError(err, "end")
  2044→	}
  2045→
  2046→	for _, s := range r.Form["match[]"] {
  2047→		matchers, err := api.parser.ParseMetricSelector(s)
  2048→		if err != nil {
  2049→			return invalidParamError(err, "match[]")
  2050→		}
  2051→		if err := api.db.Delete(r.Context(), timestamp.FromTime(start), timestamp.FromTime(end), matchers...); err != nil {
  2052→			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}
  2053→		}
  2054→	}
  2055→
  2056→	return apiFuncResult{nil, nil, nil, nil}
  2057→}

   654→func (h *Handler) isReady() bool {
   655→	return ReadyStatus(h.ready.Load()) == Ready
   656→}
   657→
   658→// Checks if server is ready, calls f if it is, returns 503 if it is not.
   659→func (h *Handler) testReady(f http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc {
   660→	return func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
   661→		switch ReadyStatus(h.ready.Load()) {
   662→		case Ready:
   663→			f(w, r)
   664→		case NotReady:
   665→			w.Header().Set("X-Prometheus-Stopping", "false")
   666→			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)
   667→			fmt.Fprintf(w, "Service Unavailable")
   668→		case Stopping:
   669→			w.Header().Set("X-Prometheus-Stopping", "true")
   670→			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusServiceUnavailable)
   671→			fmt.Fprintf(w, "Service Unavailable")
   672→		default:
   673→			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)
   674→			fmt.Fprintf(w, "Unknown state")
   675→		}
   676→	}
   677→}
   678→
   679→// Quit returns the receive-only quit channel.
   680→func (h *Handler) Quit() <-chan struct{} {
   681→	return h.quitCh
   682→}

   690→func (h *Handler) Listeners() ([]net.Listener, error) {
   691→	var listeners []net.Listener
   692→	sem := netconnlimit.NewSharedSemaphore(h.options.MaxConnections)
   693→	for _, address := range h.options.ListenAddresses {
   694→		listener, err := h.Listener(address, sem)
   695→		if err != nil {
   696→			return listeners, err
   697→		}
   698→		listeners = append(listeners, listener)
   699→	}
   700→	return listeners, nil
   701→}
   702→
   703→// Listener creates the TCP listener for web requests.
   704→func (h *Handler) Listener(address string, sem chan struct{}) (net.Listener, error) {
   705→	h.logger.Info("Start listening for connections", "address", address)
   706→
   707→	listener, err := net.Listen("tcp", address)
   708→	if err != nil {
   709→		return listener, err
   710→	}
   711→	listener = netconnlimit.SharedLimitListener(listener, sem)
   712→
   713→	// Monitor incoming connections with conntrack.
   714→	listener = conntrack.NewListener(listener,
   715→		conntrack.TrackWithName("http"),
   716→		conntrack.TrackWithTracing())
   717→
   718→	return listener, nil
   719→}
   720→
   721→// Run serves the HTTP endpoints.
   722→func (h *Handler) Run(ctx context.Context, listeners []net.Listener, webConfig string) error {
   723→	if len(listeners) == 0 {
   724→		var err error
   725→		listeners, err = h.Listeners()
   726→		if err != nil {
   727→			return err
   728→		}
   729→	}

    21→
    22→var corsHeaders = map[string]string{
    23→	"Access-Control-Allow-Headers":  "Accept, Authorization, Content-Type, Origin",
    24→	"Access-Control-Allow-Methods":  "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
    25→	"Access-Control-Expose-Headers": "Date",
    26→}
    27→
    28→// SetCORS enables cross-origin script calls.
    29→func SetCORS(w http.ResponseWriter, o *regexp.Regexp, r *http.Request) {
    30→	w.Header().Add("Vary", "Origin")
    31→	origin := r.Header.Get("Origin")
    32→	if origin == "" {
    33→		return
    34→	}
    35→
    36→	for k, v := range corsHeaders {
    37→		w.Header().Set(k, v)
    38→	}
    39→
    40→	if o.String() == "^(?:.*)$" {
    41→		w.Header().Set("Access-Control-Allow-Origin", "*")
    42→		return
    43→	}
    44→
    45→	if o.MatchString(origin) {
    46→		w.Header().Set("Access-Control-Allow-Origin", origin)
    47→	}
    48→}
    49→

92-usertext-
Search the prometheus/web directory for all Go files that might implement authentication, specifically looking for:
1. BasicAuth middleware or handlers
2. TLS client certificate validation
3. Admin API access control
4. Any middleware that validates requests
5. HTTP handler wrappers for authentication

   765→		return e

Excellent! Now I have a comprehensive understanding. Let me create a final summary document:

## Search Results Summary: Authentication Implementation in Prometheus Web Package

Based on my thorough search of the `/workspace/prometheus/web` directory, here are the findings:

### Files Analyzed
1. **`/workspace/prometheus/web/web.go`** - Main web handler (961 lines)
2. **`/workspace/prometheus/web/api/v1/api.go`** - API v1 implementation (2321 lines)
3. **`/workspace/prometheus/web/federate.go`** - Federation endpoint (376 lines)
4. **`/workspace/prometheus/web/web_test.go`** - Web handler tests
5. Various test helper files

### 1. BasicAuth Middleware and Handlers
**Finding**: BasicAuth validation is **NOT** implemented within the web package itself. Instead, it's delegated to the **prometheus/exporter-toolkit/web** library.

**Location**: `/workspace/prometheus/web/web.go` (Line 760)
```go
errCh <- toolkit_web.ServeMultiple(listeners, httpSrv, &toolkit_web.FlagConfig{WebConfigFile: &webConfig}, h.logger)
```

**Configuration**: `/workspace/prometheus/cmd/prometheus/main.go` (Line 401-404)
```go
webConfig := a.Flag(
    "web.config.file",
    "[EXPERIMENTAL] Path to configuration file that can enable TLS or authentication.",
).Default("").String()
```

The web config file is passed to `toolkit_web.ServeMultiple()` which handles TLS and authentication externally.

### 2. TLS Client Certificate Validation
**Finding**: TLS client certificate validation is also handled by the **prometheus/exporter-toolkit/web** library, not in the Prometheus web package.

**Evidence**: The `toolkit_web.FlagConfig` struct accepts a `WebConfigFile` parameter that enables:
- TLS configuration
- Client certificate validation
- BasicAuth credentials

### 3. Admin API Access Control
**Location**:

## Summary

I've created `/workspace/answer.json` with findings on three key authentication control mechanisms in prometheus/prometheus:

### **1. Admin API Access Control** (In-Repository Implementation)
Located in `web/api/v1/api.go`, the system implements access control for admin endpoints:
- **Functions**: `deleteSeries`, `snapshot`, `cleanTombstones`
- **Mechanism**: Each function checks the `enableAdmin` boolean flag
- **Endpoints**: `/admin/tsdb/delete_series`, `/admin/tsdb/clean_tombstones`, `/admin/tsdb/snapshot`
- **Response**: Returns HTTP 503 "admin APIs disabled" when `enableAdmin=false`

### **2. BasicAuth Middleware & TLS Client Certificates** (External Integration)
Delegated to the `prometheus/exporter-toolkit/web` package:
- **Configuration**: Via `webConfig` parameter in `cmd/prometheus/main.go` (lines 401-404)
- **Integration Point**: `web/web.go` line 760 - `toolkit_web.ServeMultiple()`
- **Features**: Handles TLS configuration, BasicAuth validation, and client certificate verification

### **3. Security Middleware** (In-Repository Implementation)
Supporting authentication controls in `web/web.go`:
- **`testReady` function** (line 659): Ensures server is ready before processing requests
- **`withStackTracer` function** (line 123): Implements panic recovery with security logging
- **`wrap`/`wrapAgent` functions** (api/v1/api.go lines 393-423): Request validation and CORS handling

The answer file includes complete file paths, relevant symbols, execution chains, and a detailed narrative explaining how these components work together to secure the Prometheus web UI.

 640\u2192\n   641\u2192// SetReady sets the ready status of our web Handler.\n   642\u2192func (h *Handler) SetReady(v ReadyStatus) {\n   643\u2192\tif v == Ready {\n 689\u2192// Listeners creates the TCP listeners for web requests.\n   690\u2192func (h *Handler) Listeners() ([]net.Listener, error) {\n   691\u2192\tvar listeners []net.Listener\n   692\u2192\tsem := nil\n   701\u2192}\n   702\u2192\n   703\u2192// Listener creates the TCP listener for web requests.\n   704\u2192func (h *Handler) Listener(address string, sem chan struct{}) (net.Listener, error) 718\u2192\treturn listener, nil\n   719\u2192}\n   720\u2192\n   721\u2192// Run serves the HTTP endpoints.\n   722\u2192func (h *Handler) Run(ctx context.Context, listeners []net.Listener, webConfig  770\u2192}\n   771\u2192\n   772\u2192func (h *Handler) consoles(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n   773\u2192\tctx := r.Context()\n   774\u2192\tname := route.Param(ctx, \"filepath\")\n (api_v1.RuntimeInfo, error) {\n   852\u2192\tstatus := api_v1.RuntimeInfo{\n   853\u2192\t\tStartTime:      h.birth,\n   854\u2192\t\tCWD:            h.cwd,\n   855\u2192\t\tGoroutineCount:
